              if (!event.isEmpty) {

                        <section>
                            <h4 id="1185771-5891182" class="title articleClientType act-header" data-level="1" data-section-title="" data-magellan-destination="1185771-5891182">Articles</h4>
                            <div class="content al-article-list-group" data-section-content="">

                            <div class="al-article-items">
                                    <div class="left al-article-categories">
